/FRT/0/0/ /The World English Bible uses “Yahweh” for God’s proper name in the Old Testament. This is our best reconstruction of how this most holy name was originally pronounced./This edition translates God’s Proper Name in the Old Testament as LORD or GOD (all capitals)./
,GEN,2,4, ,Yahweh,the LORD,
